# STEP 04 GR00T finetune command gate

_2026-05-30T19:33:51Z_

## Current status

The demo run is complete and reproducible. The next executable milestone is fine-tuning, but the upstream README points to a benchmark/template configuration rather than this project’s exact task setup.

## Verified upstream shape

```bash
cd /home/zeus/content/Humanoid/Isaac-GR00T
uv run python gr00t/experiment/launch_finetune.py \
  --base-model-path nvidia/GR00T-N1.7-3B \
  --dataset-path demo_data/cube_to_bowl_5 \
  --embodiment-tag NEW_EMBODIMENT \
  --modality-config-path examples/SO100/so100_config.py \
  --num-gpus 1 \
  --output-dir /tmp/test_finetune \
  --max-steps 2000 \
  --global-batch-size 32 \
  --dataloader-num-workers 4
```

## Next requirement

Choose the embodiment-specific dataset and modality config for this thesis before running a real fine-tune on GPU.

